 1 eve rosser 's high-pitched scream rang out through the entire house , bouncing off every wall , and , like a taser applied to the spine , it brought claire out of a pleasant , drowsy cuddle with her boyfriend . 
 `` oh my god , what ? '' 
 she half jumped , half fell off the couch . 
 mortal danger was nothing new around their unofficial four-person frat house . 
 in fact , mortal danger did n't even merit a full-fledged scream these days . 
 more of a raised eyebrow .

 what ? ''

 those who read the symbol do so at their peril . 
 it is the spectator , and not life , that art really mirrors . 
 diversity of opinion about a work of art shows that the work is new , complex , and vital . 
 when critics disagree , the artist is in accord with himself . 
 we can forgive a man for making a useful thing as long as he does not admire it . 
 the only excuse for making a useless thing is that one admires it intensely . 
 all art is quite useless .
